  ggl_pair_cells_/5 - apply ggl_op_ to corresponding cells of two rows
  ggl_pair_/5    - apply pairwise cell operation to two grids
  ggl_count_/3   - count occurrences of a value in a list
  ggl_unique_/2  - collect unique elements of a list
  ggl_max_pair_/2 - find the Count-V pair with highest Count
  ggl_mode_/3    - find most frequent value if count > threshold
  ggl_mask_rows_/5 - apply mask row by row
  ggl_mask_cells_/5 - apply mask cell by cell
  ggl_if_rows_/5 - apply conditional row by row
  ggl_if_cells_/5 - apply conditional cell by cell

ARCH-221: gridchain Pack (gch_*, Layer 234)

Location: packs/gridchain/
Files: pack.pl, prolog/gridchain.pl, test/test_gridchain.pl
Module: gridchain
Exports: gch_pairs/2, gch_window/3, gch_zip/3, gch_take/3, gch_drop/3,
         gch_nth/3, gch_all_same/1, gch_dedup/2, gch_cycle/3,
         gch_interleave/3, gch_split_at/4, gch_reverse/2,
         gch_diff_counts/3, gch_changes_mask/4
Dependencies: library(lists) - member/2, nth0/3, reverse/2, last/2, append/3
Layer: 234 (above gridlogic Layer 233)

Design notes:
- gch_pairs and gch_window use findall + nth0 indexing; deterministic by construction.
- gch_zip and gch_interleave use cuts on the two empty-list base clauses to prevent
  choicepoint warnings.
- gch_all_same uses cuts on the [] and [_] base clauses.
- gch_dedup uses an accumulator (Seen list) in the same pattern as gmp_unique_ordered_.
- gch_take and gch_drop clamp to actual length with min/2 rather than failing.
- gch_diff_counts delegates to gch_pairs and a recursive cell-diff helper with a cut
  on the matching-value clause.
- gch_changes_mask compares only first vs. last (using last/2), not all consecutive
  pairs, for a clean single-pass result.

ARCH-222: gridblend Pack (gbld_*, Layer 235)

Location: packs/gridblend/
Files: pack.pl, prolog/gridblend.pl, test/test_gridblend.pl
Module: gridblend
Exports: gbld_overlay/4, gbld_underlay/4, gbld_stencil/4, gbld_priority/3,
         gbld_checker_blend/5, gbld_stripe_blend/5, gbld_threshold_replace/5,
         gbld_merge_many/3, gbld_dominant/3, gbld_composite/4
Dependencies: library(lists) - member/2, nth0/3; msort/2 as built-in
Layer: 235 (above gridchain Layer 234)

Design notes:
- gbld_overlay and gbld_underlay use symmetric recursive helpers (overlay_rows_,
  underlay_rows_) that differ only in which grid's cell wins over the other.
- gbld_stencil uses SC (StencilColor) as both the trigger (mask=SC → pass source)
  and the fill value (mask/=SC → output SC), keeping the API minimal.
- gbld_priority folds the grid list right-to-left: last grid becomes the base,
  then each preceding grid is overlaid on top. First grid is topmost.
- gbld_merge_many folds left-to-right: first grid is the base; each subsequent
  grid overlays the accumulated result. Last grid is topmost.
- gbld_checker_blend passes Bg for API consistency but does not use it in cell
  selection; cell values are taken directly from one of the two input grids.
- gbld_dominant uses msort + run-length scan (gbld_best_run_/6) to find the mode.
- gbld_composite dispatches via a three-clause definition with cuts on each Mode.

ARCH-223: gridextract Pack (gxt_*, Layer 236)

Location: packs/gridextract/
Files: pack.pl, prolog/gridextract.pl, test/test_gridextract.pl
Module: gridextract
Exports: gxt_nonbg_cells/3, gxt_color_cells/3, gxt_bbox/4, gxt_crop_bbox/5,
         gxt_object_at/5, gxt_all_colors/3, gxt_color_count/4,
         gxt_largest_color/3, gxt_smallest_color/3, gxt_centered_crop/5,
         gxt_row_cells/4, gxt_col_cells/4, gxt_region_count/4, gxt_registry/3
Dependencies: library(lists) - member/2, last/2; msort/2, nth0/3, sumlist/2 as built-ins
Layer: 236 (above gridblend Layer 235)

Design notes:
- All cell-collection predicates use findall with between/3 and nth0/3 for clean,
  deterministic row-major iteration.
- gxt_bbox/4 fails on all-bg grids rather than returning a degenerate bbox.
- gxt_object_at uses iterative BFS (worklist) with member-based visited tracking.
  Suitable for the small grids (≤30×30) found in benchmark tasks.
- gxt_region_count uses the same BFS, then subtracts visited cells from the
  remaining cell list using gxt_subtract_. The if-then-else in gxt_region_count
  uses the form (Cells=[] -> ... ; ...) with Cells bound BEFORE the if-then-else
  to ensure Cells is available in the else branch.
- gxt_centered_crop uses sumlist/2 (SWI-Prolog built-in) for sum computation and
  clamps the crop window with max/min arithmetic.
- gxt_registry produces obj(Color,Count,BBox) records sorted by color via
  gxt_all_colors which uses gxt_sorted_unique_ (msort + consecutive dedup).

ARCH-224: gridgrav Pack (Layer 237)
File: packs/gridgrav/prolog/gridgrav.pl
Module: gridgrav
Exports: gra_fall_down/3, gra_fall_up/3, gra_fall_left/3, gra_fall_right/3,
         gra_fall/4, gra_col_nonbg/4, gra_row_nonbg/4, gra_set_col_bottom/5,
         gra_set_col_top/5, gra_set_row_left/5, gra_set_row_right/5,
         gra_blocked_fall/5, gra_is_settled/2, gra_gravity_score/3
Dependencies: library(lists) - member/2
Layer: 237 (above gridextract Layer 236)

Design notes:
- gra_settle_segment_/4 is the single private helper that powers all eight
  directional operations (fall_* and blocked_fall segments). Dir=down/right packs
  values to the end of a segment; Dir=up/left packs to the start.
- gra_cols_to_grid_/3 transposes a list of settled column lists back to row-major
  form using a findall+member+nth0 pattern.
- gra_split_at_first_/4 splits a list at the first occurrence of BlockColor, used
  by gra_segment_apply_ to break a column or row into independent gravity segments.
- gra_is_settled/2 is implemented as gra_fall_down(Grid,Bg,Grid): if the result
  unifies with the original, the grid is already settled.
- gra_gravity_score/3 counts positions where Grid and its fall_down result differ;
  a score of 2*N indicates N cells would move.

ARCH-225: gridstamp Pack (Layer 238, gst_*)

Layer: 238
Module: gridstamp
File: packs/gridstamp/prolog/gridstamp.pl
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2]; SWI-Prolog built-ins only.
Public predicates (14):
  gst_canvas/4, gst_stamp/6, gst_stamp_all/5, gst_scatter/5,
  gst_find_matches/4, gst_stamp_count/4, gst_pad/5, gst_unpad/3,
  gst_replicate_h/4, gst_replicate_v/4, gst_border/5, gst_center/5,
  gst_extract/6, gst_replace/5
Private helpers (3):
  gst_min_list_/2, gst_max_list_/2 (bounding box for gst_unpad)
  gst_matches_at_/5 (negation-as-failure cell match for gst_find_matches)

Design notes:
- gst_stamp uses transparency: only non-bg Stamp cells are collected as Mods;
  bg cells in Stamp leave the underlying Grid cell unchanged.
- gst_replace is opaque: all Patch cells overwrite regardless of color.
- gst_center uses direct cell bounds arithmetic (no nested stamp call) to
  avoid over-writing bg content already present in Grid.
- gst_find_matches uses gst_matches_at_ with \+ to short-circuit on first
  differing cell, making match rejection fast.
- gst_replicate_v: findall(Row, (between(1,N,_), member(Row,Grid)), Result)
  -- idiomatic repeat via backtracking over member, no explicit list concat.
- gst_border: T=0 edge case returns Grid unchanged because findall over
  between(1,0,_) yields zero rows/cells.

ARCH-226: gridalign Pack (Layer 239, gal_*)

Layer: 239
Module: gridalign
File: packs/gridalign/prolog/gridalign.pl
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2]; SWI-Prolog built-ins only
  (uses min_list/2, max_list/2, sumlist/2, list_to_set/2 from lists).
Public predicates (14):
  gal_center_of_mass/3, gal_nonbg_bbox/3, gal_bbox_center/3,
  gal_translate/5, gal_overlap_count/4, gal_overlap_score/4, gal_iou/4,
  gal_find_offset/5, gal_align_centers/4, gal_align_bbox_centers/4,
  gal_nonbg_offset/4, gal_place_at/6, gal_anchor_to/8, gal_match_any_offset/4
Private helpers (3):
  gal_nonbg_cells_/3, gal_floor_avg_/2, gal_grid_size_/3,
  gal_pick_best_offset_/6

Design notes:
- gal_iou uses \+(V1=Bg, V2=Bg) for the union condition rather than
  (V1\=Bg ; V2\=Bg). The disjunction form causes findall to backtrack over
  both branches for cells where both V1 and V2 are non-bg, double-counting
  them. The negation form is deterministic.
- gal_find_offset works on non-bg cell sets (not full grids) for efficiency:
  shift S2 by (DR,DC), count intersections with S1. No gal_translate call needed.
- gal_match_any_offset uses list_to_set to deduplicate: multiple Grid2 non-bg
  cells may produce the same offset independently.
- gal_pick_best_offset_ is a tail-recursive fold that maintains the current best
  overlap and offset; ties resolved by Manhattan distance.
- gal_place_at is transparent (same model as gridstamp's gst_stamp).
- gal_anchor_to/8 computes R0 = QR - PR, C0 = QC - PC and delegates to
  gal_place_at/6. This is the correct formula for "place Grid2 at a position
  where its cell (PR,PC) aligns with Canvas cell (QR,QC)".


ARCH-227: gridcolorop Pack (gco_*, Layer 240)

Pack name: gridcolorop
Layer: 240
Prefix: gco_
Module file: packs/gridcolorop/prolog/gridcolorop.pl
Test file: packs/gridcolorop/test/test_gridcolorop.pl
Pack file: packs/gridcolorop/pack.pl
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2] only. No cross-pack dependencies.
Work Package: WP-261

Public predicates (14):
  gco_color_counts/3, gco_distinct_colors/3, gco_nth_color/4,
  gco_count_distinct/3, gco_swap/5, gco_replace/5, gco_apply_map/4,
  gco_keep_only/4, gco_remove_color/4, gco_cycle/5, gco_rank_grid/3,
  gco_apply_palette/4, gco_most_least/4, gco_invert/4

Private helpers (5):
  gco_cell_colors_/3, gco_count_val_/3, gco_sort_by_count_desc_/2,
  gco_nth_in_/3, gco_grid_dims_/3

Design notes:
- gco_sort_by_count_desc_ uses Neg is -N (arithmetic evaluation) to compute
  the negation key for msort. Using -N as a Prolog term creates the compound
  -(N) which sorts by functor/arity rather than numeric value, causing lower-
  count items to appear first instead of last.
- gco_cycle uses ((Idx + N) mod PLen + PLen) mod PLen to handle negative N
  correctly in SWI-Prolog where mod can return negative values.
- gco_replace replaces any color including Bg; gco_swap and gco_keep_only
  do not treat Bg specially (Bg is just another value in the cell match).
- gco_invert is binary: all non-bg -> Bg, all Bg -> FgColor. It does not
  preserve distinct non-bg colors.
- gco_apply_palette delegates to gco_apply_map after building a replace map
  from (ByFreq[K] -> Palette[K]) pairs for K < min(|Palette|, |ByFreq|).


ARCH-228: gridresize Pack (grs_*, Layer 241)

Pack name: gridresize
Layer: 241
Prefix: grs_
Module file: packs/gridresize/prolog/gridresize.pl
Test file: packs/gridresize/test/test_gridresize.pl
Pack file: packs/gridresize/pack.pl
Dependencies: built-ins only (no library imports). No cross-pack dependencies.
Work Package: WP-262

Public predicates (14):
  grs_scale_up/3, grs_scale_down/4, grs_scale_down_mode/4,
  grs_double/2, grs_halve/3, grs_resize/5, grs_tile_to/4,
  grs_crop/6, grs_border_crop/4, grs_fit_in/5, grs_embed_in/5,
  grs_grid_size/3, grs_aspect_ratio/4, grs_is_square/1

Private helpers (4):
  grs_dims_/3, grs_cell_/4, grs_count_/3, grs_mode_/2

Design notes:
- All if-then-else blocks following a grs_dims_ call are wrapped in explicit
  outer parentheses. Without them, SWI-Prolog parses the preceding comma-chain
  as part of the if-then condition, leaving H and W from grs_dims_ unbound in
  the else branch. The outer parens make the entire if-then-else a single goal
  with precedence 0, cleanly separating it from the preceding grs_dims_ call.
- grs_mode_ uses Neg is -N (arithmetic evaluation) for the sort key, not the
  compound term -N, following the same pattern established in gridcolorop.
- grs_resize uses floor integer arithmetic (R*H)//NewH rather than floating-
  point to avoid rounding issues with large grids.
- grs_fit_in uses round/1 for the scaled dimensions rather than floor/1, to
  get the best-fitting integer dimension from the float scale factor.
- grs_crop clamps indices to grid bounds rather than failing on out-of-bounds
  requests; this matches the expected behavior for imprecise crop calls.


ARCH-229: gridobj Pack (gob_*, Layer 242)

Pack name: gridobj
Layer: 242
Prefix: gob_
Module file: packs/gridobj/prolog/gridobj.pl
Test file: packs/gridobj/test/test_gridobj.pl
Pack file: packs/gridobj/pack.pl
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2, min_list/2, max_list/2,
  list_to_set/2, append/3]. No cross-pack dependencies.
Work Package: WP-263

Public predicates (14):
  gob_object_cells/4, gob_object_color/4, gob_object_size/4,
  gob_object_bbox/4, gob_object_mask/5, gob_extract_object/5,
  gob_all_objects/3, gob_object_count/3, gob_largest_object/3,
  gob_smallest_object/3, gob_flood_fill/5, gob_fill_enclosed/4,
  gob_remove_object/5, gob_move_object/7

Private helpers (5):
  gob_dims_/3, gob_cell_/4, gob_cells_bbox_/2,
  gob_bfs_/7, gob_bg_bfs_/7, gob_collect_objects_/7

Design notes:
- gob_bfs_ checks both the Visited set (\+ member in Visited) and the current
  frontier tail (\+ member in Rest) before adding a cell to NewCells. This
  ensures no cell appears twice in the frontier, even when multiple frontier
  cells have the same neighbor not yet in Visited.
- gob_collect_objects_ uses an accumulator (Seen) of cells already assigned to
  a component. It skips any cell in Seen and recursively collects the rest,
  ensuring each component is found exactly once regardless of which cell within
  it is encountered as the seed.
- gob_fill_enclosed uses gob_bg_bfs_ starting from all border Bg cells to find
  all "reachable" Bg cells. Any Bg cell not in that reachable set is fully
  enclosed and is replaced by FgColor. If no Bg cells touch the border,
  all Bg cells are enclosed.
- gob_move_object clips cells that would fall outside the grid bounds after
  translation. The original cells are always removed even if the new position
  is partially or fully out of bounds.
- gob_largest_object uses neg(Neg, Cs) keys (Neg is -Len) so msort produces
  the largest first. gob_smallest_object uses pos(Len, Cs) directly.


ARCH-230: gridgroupby Pack (ggb_*, Layer 243)

Location: packs/gridgroupby/prolog/gridgroupby.pl
Test: packs/gridgroupby/test/test_gridgroupby.pl
Module: gridgroupby
Prefix: ggb_
Layer: 243
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2, append/3]
Cross-pack input: ob(Color,Cells,BBox) terms produced by gob_all_objects/3

Exports:
  ggb_group_by_color/2, ggb_group_by_size/2, ggb_group_by_row/2,
  ggb_group_by_col/2, ggb_filter_by_color/3, ggb_filter_by_size/3,
  ggb_filter_larger/3, ggb_filter_smaller/3, ggb_sort_by_size_asc/2,
  ggb_sort_by_size_desc/2, ggb_sort_by_row/2, ggb_sort_by_col/2,
  ggb_pair_by_color/2, ggb_count_per_color/2

Design notes:
- All group-by predicates use a shared ggb_group_by_key_/3 helper that collects
  k(Key,Obj) pairs, sorts by key with msort, then collects consecutive same-key
  runs into grp(Key,ObjList) terms via ggb_collect_groups_/2 and ggb_span_key_/4.
- Key equality uses == (syntactic identity) so integer keys (sizes, rows, cols)
  compare correctly; atom keys (colors) also compare correctly.
- Descending sort uses neg(Neg,Obj) keys where Neg is -Key so msort produces
  ascending Neg order (most negative = largest original key comes first).
- ggb_pair_by_color/2 leverages ggb_group_by_color and pattern-matches on
  groups with exactly two members.
- Private helpers (ggb_obj_size_, ggb_obj_row_, ggb_obj_col_, ggb_color_key_)
  are not exported; tests must not call them directly.


ARCH-231: gridrelation Pack (grl_*, Layer 244)

Location: packs/gridrelation/prolog/gridrelation.pl
Test: packs/gridrelation/test/test_gridrelation.pl
Module: gridrelation
Prefix: grl_
Layer: 244
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2], library(aggregate) for min_list
Cross-pack input: ob(Color,Cells,BBox) terms produced by gob_all_objects/3

Exports:
  grl_touching/2, grl_adjacent/3, grl_min_distance/3, grl_above/2, grl_below/2,
  grl_left_of/2, grl_right_of/2, grl_bbox_contains/2, grl_bbox_overlap/2,
  grl_cells_overlap/2, grl_same_rows/2, grl_same_cols/2, grl_direction/3,
  grl_all_relations/3

Design notes:
- grl_touching uses cut after the first matching pair to avoid redundant solutions.
- grl_min_distance uses findall to collect all pair distances then min_list.
- grl_direction uses doubled centroid (R0+R1, C0+C1) to avoid integer division;
  this is exact and avoids rounding. Tie-breaking favors vertical (above/below).
- grl_bbox_overlap uses the standard interval-overlap test on both axes:
  two intervals [a0,a1] and [b0,b1] overlap iff a0 =< b1 and b0 =< a1.
  Note: adjacent single-cell bboxes (col 0 and col 1) do NOT overlap by this test.
- grl_all_relations uses a findall over an association list of Rel-Goal pairs.
  The list has 10 entries (all relations except grl_direction and grl_min_distance).


ARCH-232: gridtransform Pack (gtr_*, Layer 245)

Location: packs/gridtransform/prolog/gridtransform.pl
Test: packs/gridtransform/test/test_gridtransform.pl
Module: gridtransform
Prefix: gtr_
Layer: 245
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2]

Exports:
  gtr_color_map/3, gtr_apply_color_map/3, gtr_diff_cells/3, gtr_diff_count/3,
  gtr_same_cells/3, gtr_changed_colors/3, gtr_invert_map/2, gtr_compose_maps/3,
  gtr_is_identity_map/1, gtr_apply_changes/3, gtr_delta_grid/4, gtr_overlay/4,
  gtr_common_grid/4, gtr_is_color_permutation/2

Design notes:
- gtr_color_map uses sort/2 (which removes duplicates) then a consistency check.
  The consistency check \+ member(cm(VA,VB1)...), member(cm(VA,VB2)...), VB1\=VB2
  ensures no source color has two different targets.
- gtr_apply_color_map uses member/2 for the lookup; the first matching cm/2 is used.
- Color maps are lists of cm(OldColor, NewColor) terms.
- Changes are lists of chg(R, C, OldColor, NewColor) terms.
- gtr_apply_changes uses member/2; the last matching chg for a cell wins (findall
  collects one value per cell, the last chg match). For deterministic use, provide
  at most one change per cell.
- gtr_delta_grid and gtr_overlay compose: apply delta = overlay(A, delta(A,B,Bg), Bg) = B.


ARCH-233: gridobjmatch Pack (gom_*, Layer 246)

Location: packs/gridobjmatch/prolog/gridobjmatch.pl
Test: packs/gridobjmatch/test/test_gridobjmatch.pl

  gom_move_vector/2, gom_move_vectors/2, gom_constant_move/2,

  gom_same_structure/2, gom_count_change/3

Design notes:
- Operates on ob(Color, Cells, BBox) terms from gob_all_objects/3; BBox = r0(R0,C0,R1,C1).

  these detect brand-new or lost color classes, not individual objects.

ARCH-234: symtab Pack (st_*, Layer 247)

Location: packs/symtab/prolog/symtab.pl
Test: packs/symtab/test/test_symtab.pl
Module: symtab
Prefix: st_
Layer: 247
Dependencies: library(lists) [member/2, subtract/3, numlist/3], library(apply) [maplist/2-3, include/3], library(aggregate) [aggregate_all/3]

Exports:
  st_build_table/2, st_identify_symbols/2, st_contrastive_learn/2,
  st_apply_table/3, st_hole_count/2, st_lookup/3,
  st_entry_consistent/2, st_color_feature/2, st_size_feature/2,
  st_position_feature/3, st_is_symbol/2, st_candidate_symbols/2,
  st_score_table/3, st_best_table/3

Design notes:
- Symbol tables are lists of sym(Feature, Value) terms. Features are color(C),
  size(N), holes(N), or pos(Q). Values are atoms (typically color atoms).
- Contrastive learning performs cross-pair analysis: for each pair, extract
  candidate sym entries, then intersect across all pairs keeping only entries
  consistent with every pair.
- st_hole_count uses a bbox-area minus cell-count approximation. For exact
  topological hole counting, a full grid-context flood fill is required.
- st_is_symbol uses size and color heuristics: smaller than all content objects,
  or a unique color not shared by content objects.
- st_best_table scores all candidate tables and returns the highest-scoring one;
  ties favor the shorter (simpler) table via msort lexicographic ordering.
- Private helpers use the trailing-underscore convention.


ARCH-235: invariant Pack (iv_*, Layer 248)

WP-278: periodfix Pack (ppf_*, Layer 253)
Location: packs/periodfix/
  prolog/periodfix.pl  - module periodfix, 14 public predicates
  test/test_periodfix.pl - 30 PLUnit tests
  pack.pl              - manifest
Layer: 253, Prefix: ppf_
Dependencies: library(lists), library(apply)
Exports: ppf_list_period/2, ppf_majority/2, ppf_tile_from_list/3,
  ppf_violations_list/4, ppf_repair_list/4, ppf_best_period_list/3,
  ppf_tile_2d/4, ppf_violations_2d/5, ppf_repair_grid/5,
  ppf_best_periods/3, ppf_single_violation_list/4, ppf_repair_single_list/4,
  ppf_single_violation_2d/5, ppf_repair_single_grid/5
Design notes:
- A list has period P if List[i] = List[i mod P] for all i.
- Majority-vote tile: modal value at each phase index (i mod P for lists, (r mod PH, c mod PW) for grids).
- ppf_best_period_list and ppf_best_periods cap search at N//2 (or H//2, W//2) to
  avoid the trivial full-length period that always reports zero violations.
- ppf_run_mode_ uses a cut after head-match clause to remain deterministic.
- ppf_single_violation_* predicates guarantee exactly one corruption; they fail on 0 or 2+.
- No cross-pack dependencies.

ARC-AGI-2 WAVE 7 ARCHITECTURE NOTE - STAIRCASE LIFT

Location: src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl, Wave 7 block.
Implements: arc2_named_rule(staircase_lift), arc2_transform(staircase_lift, +Grid, -Result),
            arc2_induce_rule(+TrainingPairs, staircase_lift).
Solves: task 4c3d4a41 (8x20 staircase-bar repositioning).

Architecture: the rule reads two independent regions of the input grid.
Left half (cols 0-8): staircase pattern; odd columns 1,3,5,7 encode heights.
Right half (cols 9-19): rectangular frame with four color bars at odd cols.
The staircase heights directly constrain where each color bar ends in the output
(MaxEnd = 5 - H), with bar length clipped to fit the available space.
Output left half is cleared; output right half is rebuilt from the bar descriptors.

Helper predicates (private to arc_benchmark_2 module):
  arc2_sl_col_h_/3, arc2_sl_count_up_/5, arc2_sl_bar_/4,
  arc2_sl_first_color_/5, arc2_sl_run_len_/5, arc2_sl_out_/4, arc2_sl_val_/4.
No new Data Layer pack is required; the rule is self-contained within the benchmark.
Score impact: 6/120 = 5.00% -> 7/120 = 5.83% (+1 task, +0.83%).


ARC-AGI-2 WAVE 13 ARCHITECTURE NOTE - ODD COL

Location: src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl, Wave 13 block (after Wave 12 waterfall block).
Implements: arc2_named_rule(odd_col), arc2_transform(odd_col, +Grid, -Result),
            arc2_induce_rule(+TrainingPairs, odd_col).
Solves: task 38007db0 (tiled grid with one unique cell per row section).

Architecture: the rule detects uniform separator rows and cols, builds a
row-section by col-section partition, then votes per row section to find
the col section whose interior strip is the odd one out. The output grid
has the same row count as the input but the column width of one col section.

Key predicates (private to arc_benchmark_2 module):
  oc_all_same_/2           - all elements of a list equal one value
  oc_adjacent_pairs_/2     - turn a list into adjacent pairs
  oc_strip_/4              - slice a list from index C0 to C1 inclusive
  oc_strips_for_row_/4     - extract one strip per col section for a row
  oc_majority_strip_/2     - compute majority value at each position across strips
  oc_find_unique_idx_/3    - find the one strip index that differs from majority
  oc_vote_unique_col_/5    - vote for the unique col section in one row section
  oc_build_secs_/5         - emit rows for each section using the voted col section

No new Data Layer pack is required; all logic is self-contained in the benchmark file.
Score impact: 12/120 = 10.00% -> 13/120 = 10.83% (+1 task, +0.83%).

-- ARC-AGI-2 Wave 14: reflect_axis --

Location: src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl, Wave 14 block (after Wave 13 odd_col block).
Implements: arc2_named_rule(reflect_axis), arc2_transform(reflect_axis, +Grid, -Result),
            arc2_induce_rule(+TrainingPairs, reflect_axis).
Solves: task 7ed72f31 (shapes reflected across nearest 2-marker axis).

Architecture: the rule finds the background color by mode of the grid, groups
2-cells into 4-connected clusters, groups non-background non-2 cells into
4-connected shape components, pairs each shape with its nearest 2-cluster by
minimum Manhattan distance, determines the axis type (point/vertical/horizontal)
from the cluster's geometry, then reflects each shape cell and adds the result
to the output grid.

Key predicates (private to arc_benchmark_2 module):
  ra_bg_/2                 - background color by mode
  ra_nrc_/3                - grid dimensions
  ra_inb_/4                - bounds check
  ra_nbrs4_/5              - 4-connected neighbors
  ra_absorb_/4             - BFS frontier absorption
  ra_bfs4_/6               - 4-connected BFS over point sets
  ra_cc4_/4                - connected components of R-C pairs
  ra_split_col_/4          - split cells by color
  ra_add_col_/3            - add color to R-C pairs
  ra_shape_comps_/5        - shape connected components
  ra_min_manhattan_/3      - minimum Manhattan distance
  ra_nearest_cluster_/3    - nearest 2-cluster for a shape
  ra_extract_rows_/2       - extract row indices from R-C pairs
  ra_extract_cols_/2       - extract col indices from R-C pairs
  ra_all_equal_/1          - check all list elements equal
  ra_axis_/2               - axis type from 2-cluster geometry
  ra_reflect_/5            - reflect point through axis
  ra_set_cell_/5           - set one cell in a grid
  ra_reflect_pts_/7        - add reflected cells to grid
  ra_apply_refls_/6        - reflect all shape components

No new Data Layer pack is required; all logic is self-contained in the benchmark file.
Score impact: 13/120 = 10.83% -> 14/120 = 11.67% (+1 task, +0.83%).

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 15: period_repair - Periodic-pattern deviation repair (task 135a2760).
Finds inner sequences between wall markers in rows and columns. For each sequence,
selects the period P (in 2..N//2) with minimum-support >= 0.75 and fewest errors (1..3),
then repairs deviating cells to the majority-vote base. Row repair first, then column
repair via transpose-repair-transpose. New predicates:
  pr2_repair_row_/3        - repair one row by segment
  pr2_fix_segs_/3          - iterate over wall-pair segments
  pr2_extract_/4           - extract sub-list
  pr2_apply_fixes_/4       - apply error corrections to row
  pr2_replace_nth0_/4      - replace element at index
  pr2_best_period_/4       - select best period with support threshold
  pr2_majority_base_/3     - majority-vote base for all residues
  pr2_min_support_/4       - minimum support fraction across residues
  pr2_errors_/4            - collect deviating positions
  pr2_mode_/2              - mode of a list
  pr2_mode_acc_/6          - mode accumulator helper

No new Data Layer pack is required; all logic is self-contained in the benchmark file.
Score impact: 14/120 = 11.67% -> 15/120 = 12.50% (+1 task, +0.83%).

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 16: legend_fill - Frame-interior fill from color lookup table (task dbff022c).
A compact legend table (solid 2xN or Nx2 block of distinct non-background rows or columns)
maps frame-border colors to fill colors. Enclosed interior cells of frames whose border color
is a legend key are filled with the corresponding value. Key direction is determined by
counting frame-color matches in each legend row or column. Flood-fill from the grid boundary
finds enclosed background cells; uniqueness of adjacent non-background color assigns each
enclosed cell to its containing frame. New predicates:
  lf_legend_/4              - find legend and return key/value lists
  lf_best_block_/4          - find longest non-identical solid 2xN or Nx2 block
  lf_row_block_/5           - solid block in adjacent row pair (max-length run)
  lf_col_block_/5           - solid block in adjacent column pair (max-length run)
  lf_solid_run_/7           - enumerate all starting positions of solid runs
  lf_solid_end_/6           - extend solid run to its end
  lf_orient_kv_/6           - determine key vs value direction by frame-color matching
  lf_enclosed_all_/3        - BFS flood fill from boundary; return enclosed Bg cells
  lf_flood_/7               - iterative BFS through Bg cells
  lf_frame_colors_/4        - non-Bg colors adjacent to any enclosed cell
  lf_apply_fill_/5          - fill enclosed cells for one key color
  lf_enclosed_for_color_/4  - enclosed cells whose unique frame color is K
  lf_unique_frame_color_/5  - all non-Bg 4-neighbors equal K
  lf_fill_grid_/4           - apply cell value replacements to the grid
  lf_take_/4                - extract sub-list of length Len starting at Start
  lf_extract_col_/3         - extract all values in column C from Grid

No new Data Layer pack required; all logic is self-contained in arc_benchmark_2.pl.
Score impact: 15/120 = 12.50% -> 16/120 = 13.33% (+1 task, +0.83%).

WP-279: iochan Pack (ic_*, Layer 254)

- iochan is independent of the tooling pack; tooling may wrap iochan channels as
  tools via pai_tool_register/2 but iochan has no internal dependency on tooling.

WP-283 bar_extend (Layer 258):
  Location: Mentova/src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl
  Layer 258 in the ARC-AGI-2 solver stack.
  Depends on: arc2_named_rule/1, arc2_transform/3 dispatch framework.
  Exports: arc2_transform(bar_extend, +Grid, -Out).
  The rule is self-contained: divider detection, bar analysis, period
  construction, and right-side fill are all local to the bar_extend block.

WP-284 straighten_diag (Layer 259) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 26
  Layer 259 in the ARC-AGI-2 solver stack.
  Depends on: arc2_named_rule/1, arc2_transform/3 dispatch framework,
              arc2_bg_color_/2, arc2_cell_/4, arc2_set_cell_/5.
  Exports: arc2_transform(straighten_diag, +Grid, -Out).
  The rule is self-contained: diagonal detection, 8-connected component
  finding, anchor analysis, gap scanning, grid rebuild, and perpendicular
  stub pruning are all local to the straighten_diag block.
  Key design choice: stub pruning is restricted to DiagNbr (cells originally
  8-adjacent to diagonal cells) so that genuine line endpoints are never
  removed. This prevents over-pruning in grids with T-junctions and
  endpoints in the orthogonal tree.

WP-285 stream_extend (Layer 260) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 27
  Layer 260 in the ARC-AGI-2 solver stack.
  Depends on: arc2_named_rule/1, arc2_transform/3 dispatch framework,
              arc2_bg_color_/2, arc2_cell_/4, arc2_set_cell_/5.
  Exports: arc2_transform(stream_extend, +Grid, -Out).
  The rule is self-contained: A-marker component detection (4-connected
  flood-fill), seed chain collection, and periodic extension fill are
  all local to the stream_extend block (arc2_sx_* predicates).
  Key design choice: each cardinal direction is tried independently per
  component via arc2_sx_try_dir_/8 with cut-on-success, so a direction
  that yields no valid chains fails cleanly without side effects.
  Chain collection terminates at BG (signals extension needed) or fails
  when hitting the grid boundary or another marker cell. Extension uses
  foldl over a findall-collected fill list to accumulate grid mutations
  without destructive assignment.

WP-286 slide_open (Layer 261) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 28
  Layer 261 in the ARC-AGI-2 solver stack.
  Depends on: arc2_named_rule/1, arc2_transform/3 dispatch framework,
              arc2_cell_/4, arc2_set_cell_/5.
  Exports: arc2_transform(slide_open, +Grid, -Out).
  The rule is self-contained: divider detection, 4-connected component
  finding, rightward slide to the divider, and open-row fill are all
  local to the slide_open block (arc2_so_* predicates).
  Key design choice: components are erased with placeholder 6 in a first
  foldl pass, then placed at shifted positions in a second foldl pass.
  This two-pass design prevents a shifted component from overwriting its
  own source cells in a single pass. The placeholder 6 never remains in
  the output because every erased cell is overwritten in the place pass.
  Open-row detection checks three conditions simultaneously:
    (1) cell(R, DC-1) = 0  - a gap exists adjacent to the divider,
    (2) cell(R, DC-2) != 0 - the gap is isolated (no adjacent block),
    (3) a 0-cell exists in columns 0..DC-3 - another object is present.
  Only rows satisfying all three conditions are filled right of the
  divider with value 2.

WP-287 diag_beam (Layer 262) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 29
  Layer 262 in the ARC-AGI-2 solver stack.
  Depends on: arc2_named_rule/1, arc2_transform/3 dispatch framework,
              arc2_set_cell_/5, memberchk/2.
  Exports: arc2_transform(diag_beam, +Grid, -Out).
  The rule is self-contained: pair detection, beam marching, obstacle
  bounce, and perpendicular ray extension are all local to the diag_beam
  block (arc2_db_* predicates).
  Key design choice: the original Sixes list is collected once before any
  beam fires and is used unchanged throughout. Newly placed 6-fills from
  bounce rays are not added to Sixes, so later beams see only pre-existing
  obstacles. This matches observed task behavior: each beam pair operates
  independently with respect to obstacle detection.
  The march predicate uses a base clause matching the destination (R2,C2)
  to stop cleanly without off-by-one risk.
  Bounce rays stop at the first existing 6 they encounter (no secondary
  bounce), keeping the transform single-pass and terminating.

Wave 30 - frame_absorb (WP-288, Layer 263) - Architecture Notes:
  Task d35bdbdc introduces frame blocks (3x3 squares or cross shapes) with
  a center cell and arm cells, connected by a snake path that is invariant.
  The snake (5-valued cells) must be excluded from component finding; failing
  to exclude them creates a large spurious monochrome component that would
  be incorrectly erased, corrupting the grid.
  The absorption graph is directed: edge X -> Y means X.CV = Y.AV. The graph
  is processed greedily: monochrome blocks (CV = AV) are processed first
  because they may interact with other blocks' predecessor relationships.
  Processing is recursive: each step removes 1-2 blocks and recurs, ensuring
  termination with O(N^2) complexity in the number of blocks.
  The center cell of a monochrome block is identified as the cell with the
  highest 4-connectivity degree within the component (the most-connected
  interior cell of a cross or square).
  All arc2_fa_* predicates use foldl and maplist to keep the implementation
  declarative and backtrack-safe.
  Regression: all 29 previously solved tasks continue to pass (30/30 total).

Layer 264 — shape_beam (WP-289):
Task 5961cc34. Background BG=8. Rod: value-4 head cell with value-2 trail.
Shapes: connected components of 1-cells (body) and 3-cells (exit markers).
Exit direction determined by which side of the 3-cells is open (BG).
Beam relays through shapes in sequence; each shape redirects beam.
Shapes not reached are deleted (not copied to output).

WP-290 shape_classify (Layer 265) - Wave 32, Task aa4ec2a5.
Two-color grid (background + shapes). Flood-fill BG from perimeter (4-connected)
identifies outside cells. BG cells not reached = holes (color 6). Outside BG cells
with any 8-connected non-BG neighbor = border (color 2). Shape components that
4-touch any hole are re-colored 8; all others keep their original color (1).

Layer 266 - tile_stamp (WP-291):
Task bf45cf4b. Background identified as most-frequent value in flattened grid.
Non-background cells partitioned into 4-connected components. The one component
using >1 distinct value is the kernel; all others form the indicator pattern.
Kernel bounding box extracted verbatim as kernel tile (interior BG cells kept).
Indicator pattern bounding box defines an NR x NC tile grid; non-background
positions within the bounding box are T (stamp here), background positions are F.
Output: NR*KR rows x NC*KC cols. Each tile position gets either the kernel tile
or a row of background cells, based on the indicator T/F map.

Layer 267 - rail_fill (WP-292):
Task 271d71e2. Background = Grid[0][0]. Valid box detection: 0-bordered
rectangle whose interior cells are exclusively 5 or 7. Arm detection:
scan each of 4 directions from the box boundary; the first and second
9-column (or 9-row) encountered are the inner and outer rails respectively.
arm_gap = distance between rails. fill order: column(or row)-major from
the arm side, with traversal direction designed so the first N7in cells
in the order exactly coincide with the existing 7-positions in the input
(a diagonal staircase from the arm-side near corner). N7gained = min(gap,
free_cells). New interior: first N7new cells in order become 7, rest 5.
Box shifts by N7gained toward outer rail (on the arm axis only). New inner
rail = outer + NewGap*(same sign as original inner-outer); none if NewGap=0.

WAVE 35: bbox_fill (WP-293, Layer 268)
arc2_transform(bbox_fill) pipeline:
1. arc2_bxf_legend_: scan column pairs left-to-right in bottom half; for each
   pair (LC,LC+1) find the maximal contiguous block of rows where Grid[R][LC]
   != BG; stop at first such block. Accepts rows where Grid[R][LC+1] may be BG
   (encodes V=BG = "block fill" mapping).
2. findall K-cells excluding legend cells; arc2_bxf_bbox_ computes bounding
   box; density check (NK == area -> Dense=true).
3. keysort by area ascending -> InfosAsc. Smallest bbox first in list.
4. arc2_bxf_cell_val_ dispatches:
   - Legend cell -> original value.
   - BG cell -> arc2_bxf_fill_for_ (first match in InfosAsc = smallest bbox).
   - Erase K-cell (V=0, BG!=0) -> same as BG cell.
   - Mapped K-cell, Dense=true -> fill color V.
   - Mapped K-cell, Dense=false -> original K (re-paint).
   - Unmapped non-BG -> original value.
Design notes: Sorting ascending means smallest bbox is first; first match in
arc2_bxf_fill_for_ is the tightest enclosure. This naturally implements
"smaller overrides larger" without a separate draw-order loop. V=BG fill works
because BG cells inside the smaller bbox get BG from fill_for (overriding the
fill from a larger enclosing bbox), and K-cells are re-painted on top.

WAVE 36: slide_void (WP-294, Layer 269)
arc2_transform(slide_void) pipeline:
1. arc2_svo_void_: collect all 0-cells; bounding box gives void top-left (VR,VC),
   height H, and width W.
2. arc2_svo_marker_: collect all 2-cells; bounding box gives marker top-left
   (MR,MC); H and W must match void dimensions.
3. arc2_svo_block_bfs_: BFS over block positions (top-left coordinates) starting
   at (VR,VC). arc2_svo_one_nbr_/9 determines valid slides: slide up checks row
   R-1 cols C..C+W-1; slide down checks row R+H cols C..C+W-1; slide left checks
   col C-1 rows R..R+H-1; slide right checks col C+W rows R..R+H-1. A cell is
   passable if its original value is 0 or 1.
4. arc2_svo_farthest_end_: from Reached (all R-C-Dist triples), collect non-start
   positions that are dead-ends (arc2_svo_is_deadend_: exactly 1 slide neighbour).
   msort ascending by distance; last element = farthest.
5. arc2_svo_adj_marker_: check if any face cell of the farthest dead-end is 2.
   If yes, target = (MR,MC); else target = farthest dead-end. Fallback to marker
   when no dead-end reachable.
6. Output: old void cells set to 1, target cells set to 0, rest unchanged.
Design notes: Block-movement BFS avoids cell-level explosion. Passability includes
0-cells (the void itself) so the block can slide back through its own starting
footprint. The farthest dead-end is the far end of the river maze; adjacency to
the 2-marker signals that the void should enter the marker pocket exactly.

WAVE 37: concentric_rings (WP-295, Layer 270)
Task 13e47133.
Entry point: arc2_transform(concentric_rings, Grid, Out).
Pipeline:
1. arc2_cri_bg_: flatten Grid; msort count-value pairs; last = BG.
2. arc2_cri_div_: exclude BG cells; same msort on remainder; last = Div.
3. Collect all non-Div cells; arc2_cri_comps_: flood-fill (4-connected,
   blocked by Div) partitions NDCs into a list of components.
4. For each component: collect boundary cells via arc2_cri_is_bnd_
   (grid edge OR 8-adjacent to any Div cell). Run arc2_cri_bfs_ (4-connected
   multi-source BFS from boundary set) to get a ring-distance map (R-C-D triples).
5. For each component: collect marker cells (non-BG, non-Div, exactly 1 cell in
   the component list at that ring position); build Ring-Color pairs.
   arc2_cri_build_cycle_: sort by ring, fill BG gaps, return Cycle list.
6. Output construction: maplist over rows and columns; Div cells pass through;
   each non-Div cell looks up its component CI, retrieves RM and Cycle for CI,
   gets distance D from RM, applies D mod CLen to index Cycle.
Design notes:
- 8-connectivity for ring-0 Div-adjacency vs 4-connectivity for BFS:
  This split handles L-shaped components where a Div corner creates a
  concavity; a cell diagonally adjacent to the Div corner must be ring-0 to
  produce correct ring distances in the concavity region. Using 4-connectivity
  for BFS propagation keeps ring distances consistent with rectilinear distance.
- Component-local cycles: each component can have different marker cells and
  different color sequences; cycles are built independently per component.
- BFS seeded from entire boundary simultaneously (multi-source) so ring K is
  the rectilinear distance to the nearest ring-0 cell.

WAVE 38: fill_enclosed (WP-296, Layer 271)
Component: arc_benchmark_2.pl, wave 38 block.
Design decisions:
- Connected-component approach replaces boundary-seed BFS: seeding BFS from boundary
  cells incorrectly marks boundary-flush pockets as reachable; the component approach
  correctly identifies each BG cluster regardless of boundary proximity.
- FrameSet derived from VAdj-adjacent values: avoids including outer-wall values (like
  the 1-cells in P3 that separate interior from exterior) in the frame set.
- FOthers requires a pure-frame structural test: a value V is a legitimate alternative
  frame color only if it ALONE forms a complete enclosure around some BG component.
  This separates multi-frame pockets (P1) from contamination tokens (test case value 0).
- VDec fallback coverage: VDecContam (from FSAdj) plus any remaining non-standard values
  ensures contamination detection works even when VDec cells are not adjacent to VAdj.
- Background disconnection handled by finding ALL BG components: in P4 the path (1-cells)
  splits the background into two regions; neither region passes the pocket test (1 not
  in FrameSet) so only the true 2x2 pocket is identified.
- Fallback FrameSet (empty FSAdj): when VAdj cells are surrounded only by BG cells
  (P4-style), fall back to all non-BG/M/VAdj values; in P4 this gives {2} = the frame.
- List-based BFS (no dynamic facts): consistent with existing file style; adequate
  performance for 30x30 grids (~0.6s total for all 4 training pairs + test case).

WAVE 39: room_outline (WP-297, Layer 272)
Task 8f3a5a89.
Entry point: arc2_transform(room_outline, Grid, Out).
Pipeline:
1. arc2_ro_seed_: nth0 row-major scan for the unique 6-cell; returns SR, SC.
2. arc2_ro_flood_ / arc2_ro_bfs_: 4-connected BFS from (SR,SC) through
   value-8 cells; result msorted into Vis.
3. arc2_ro_keep_walls_: findall collects all non-8 non-6 positions (WallCells);
   arc2_ro_wall_comps_ partitions into 4-connected components via arc2_ro_wbfs_;
   include/3 retains components where once((member, arc2_ro_adj4_vis_)) succeeds;
   append/2 flattens to WallKeep.
4. arc2_ro_bdry_walls_: re-partitions WallKeep via arc2_ro_wall_comps_;
   retains only components where once((member(R-C,Comp), (R=0;R=NR1;C=0;C=NC1)))
   succeeds; appends to BdryWalls.
5. Output via maplist/numlist double loop: arc2_ro_cell_out_ classifies each
   cell as seed / perimeter (7) / interior (8) / kept-wall / erased-wall (8).
6. arc2_ro_is_perim_: grid-edge cells pass immediately (cut); interior cells
   pass if any of the 8 surrounding in-bounds positions is in BdryWalls.
Design notes:
- Component-based wall filter (step 3) correctly handles deep staircase cells
  that have no direct accessible 4-neighbour but belong to a component that
  does touch Vis elsewhere.
- Boundary-connected wall filter (step 4) correctly handles floating island
  walls inside the room; cells 8-adjacent to a floating island are interior,
  not perimeter.
- Two-phase component calculation ensures erased wall cells (not in WallKeep)
  do not contribute to BdryWalls and do not generate perimeter cells.
- arc2_ro_wbfs_: BFS maintains an Avail list of unassigned wall cells;
  subtract/3 removes newly discovered cells from Avail to prevent revisiting.

WAVE 44: jigsaw_fill (WP-302, Layer 277) — 2026-07-01
Layer: 277 (ARC-AGI-2 reasoning layer).
Module: arc_benchmark_2.pl (Mentova games layer).
Rule name: jigsaw_fill.

Structural pattern: the input grid encodes a spatial puzzle where a 2-color
  template (with "holes") and a multi-color objects region (with "pieces") are
  laid side-by-side or top-to-bottom. The pieces exactly tile the holes.

Split detection architecture: four candidate split strategies are tried in
  order — row-split-top, row-split-bottom, col-split-left, col-split-right.
  Each is validated by checking (1) template has exactly 2 colors and (2) hole
  cell count equals piece cell count.

Piece extraction: BFS from unvisited non-background cells. Multi-color pieces
  are represented as lists of R-C-V triples (row, col, value) so per-cell colors
  are preserved through normalization and placement.

Exact cover solver: a fewest-placements-first heuristic ensures the most
  constrained pieces are placed first, reducing backtracking to near zero.
  Color map accumulates (R-C)-Color assignments; applied to template in a
  final maplist pass.

Integration: arc2_named_rule(jigsaw_fill) registers the rule for generic
  arc2_benchmark_run/3 dispatch. No external modules required.

Data flow:
  Grid -> find_split -> (Tmpl, Hole, ObjGrid, ObjBg)
       -> holes(Tmpl) -> Holes
       -> pieces(ObjGrid) -> Pieces
       -> augment(Pieces, Holes) -> PiecesWP
       -> msort -> Sorted
       -> cover(Sorted, Holes) -> ColorMap
       -> apply(Tmpl, ColorMap) -> Out

Score: 41/120 = 34.17% -> 42/120 = 35.00%.
Acc_342. SPARC: Specification v274, Pseudocode v266, Architecture v267,
  Refinement v326, Completion v332.

       -> build_out_(Pockets2) -> Out

WAVE 46: two_join (WP-304, Layer 279) — 2026-07-01
Task 20270e3b. Two 4-objects joined at 7 markers.

Component: arc2_transform(two_join, Grid, Out)
  Located in: Mentova/src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl
  Entry predicate: arc2_named_rule(two_join) + arc2_transform(two_join)

Sub-components:
  arc2_tj_nonbg_pos_ / arc2_tj_row_nonbg_
    -- collect all non-1 R-C positions from the grid
  arc2_tj_all_sevens_ / arc2_tj_row_sevens_
    -- collect all 7-cell R-C positions
  arc2_tj_seven_clusters_ / arc2_tj_grow_cluster_
    -- split 7-cells into two 4-connected clusters G1 and G2
  arc2_tj_seven_nbrs_ / arc2_tj_filter_adj_
    -- BFS neighbors within the 7-cell set
  arc2_tj_bfs_obj_ / arc2_tj_bfs_exp_
    -- BFS through all non-1 cells from a seed set
  arc2_tj_adj_nbrs_ / arc2_tj_nbr_filt_
    -- in-bounds non-1 neighbors for BFS expansion
  arc2_tj_subtract_pos_
    -- set subtraction: AllPos minus ObjA gives ObjB
  arc2_tj_shift_ / arc2_tj_min_row_ / arc2_tj_min_col_
    -- compute dr = minR(base)-minR(shift)-1, dc = minC(base)-minC(shift)
  arc2_tj_shift_pos_
    -- apply (dr, dc) shift to all positions in ObjB
  arc2_tj_valid_pos_
    -- verify all shifted positions have non-negative row and col
  arc2_tj_combined_size_ / arc2_tj_max_row_ / arc2_tj_max_col_
    -- compute merged bounding box area for ordering selection
  arc2_tj_build_out_ / arc2_tj_make_grid_ / arc2_tj_make_row_
    -- construct output grid: merged positions -> 4, background -> 1

Data flow:
  Grid -> nonbg_pos_ -> AllPos
       -> all_sevens_ -> Sevens -> seven_clusters_ -> G1, G2
  For each ordering (base_7, shift_7):
    bfs_obj_(base_7, AllPos) -> ObjA
    AllPos - ObjA -> ObjB
    shift_(base_7, shift_7) -> (dr, dc)
    shift_pos_(ObjB, dr, dc) -> ObjBs
    IF valid_pos_(ObjBs): size = combined_size_(ObjA, ObjBs)
  Pick min-size ordering -> FinalA, FinalBs
  build_out_(FinalA, FinalBs) -> Out

  Positions stored as R-C pairs throughout.

WP-306: stamp_grid (Layer 281, Task dfadab01)
Design: The rule decomposes input into three classes of cells:
  (1) SHAPE cells: a single non-background color with a 4x4 tight bounding box.
      These are erased in the output.
  (2) DEFINITION MARKER: the single cell at (SR1+1, SC1+1) - it links shape to
      stamp type and is skipped.
  (3) PLACEMENT MARKERS: all other non-background cells; each triggers a stamp.
  When no shape is present, all non-background cells are placement markers.
Layer division:
  arc2_sg_bg_/arc2_sg_run_: background detection (mode of sorted flat list)
  arc2_sg_shape_: find 4x4 tight-bbox color cluster
  arc2_sg_mval_: pattern matching (offset cells = SC, non-offset cells != SC)
  arc2_sg_mkrs_: marker collection with exclusion predicates
  arc2_sg_cell_: per-cell output lookup (member/3 over markers and offsets)
  arc2_transform(stamp_grid): top-level orchestration via maplist
Key insight: non-offset cells in the shape bbox need NOT be background;
  they may contain placement markers (e.g. P2 training pair). The shape
  identification requires only that offset cells hold the shape color and
  non-offset cells do not.
All positions are 0-indexed (nth0). Output uses maplist with lambda closures.
  Pairs_keys/pairs_values used for bbox computation from findall R-C pairs.

Score: 45/120 = 37.50% -> 46/120 = 38.33%.
Acc_346. SPARC: Specification v274, Pseudocode v270, Architecture v271,
  Refinement v330, Completion v336.

WP-307: layout_stack (Layer 282, Task 291dc1e1)
Architecture:

Component: arc2_ls_corner_ (Grid, CR, CC)
  Purpose: Locate the unique corner cell containing value 0.
  Strategy: Try all four corner (row,col) pairs; first match wins.
  Output: (CR, CC) = indices of the 0-corner.

Component: arc2_ls_mode_ (Grid, CR, CC, Mode, PrimReverse, SecReverse)
  Purpose: Read the adjacent cell in the header row to determine mode.
  Strategy: If AdjVal=1, mode=row_major; if AdjVal=2, mode=col_major.
    PrimReverse = (CR == last_row). SecReverse = (CC == last_col).
  Output: Mode, PrimReverse, SecReverse booleans.

Component: arc2_ls_interior_ (Grid, CR, CC, Interior)
  Purpose: Strip header row and col to expose the content area.
  Strategy: Delete row CR, then maplist-delete col CC from each row.
  Output: Interior grid with header row and col removed.

Component: arc2_ls_col_bands_ / arc2_ls_row_bands_ (Interior, Bands)
  Purpose: Find bands of consecutive active (non-8) columns or rows.
  Strategy: include/3 selects active indices; arc2_ls_consec_groups_
    partitions into consecutive runs.
  Output: List of bands, each a list of consecutive indices.

Component: arc2_ls_band_stretches_ / arc2_ls_band_col_stretches_
  Purpose: Within a band, find maximal consecutive active sub-ranges.
  Strategy: Same include/consec_groups_ approach; extract sub-grids.
  Output: List of sub-grids (stretches).

Component: arc2_ls_rotate_ccw_ (Grid, Rotated)
  Purpose: Rotate a grid 90 degrees counter-clockwise.
  Strategy: Output row i = input column C-1-i read top-to-bottom.
    Implemented as maplist over column indices.
  Output: Rotated grid (H x W -> W x H).

Component: arc2_ls_center_block_ (MaxW, Block, Centered)
  Purpose: Pad each row of a block with 8s to reach MaxW columns.
  Strategy: Pad = (MaxW-W)//2 left, Pad2 = MaxW-W-Pad right.
  Output: Each row padded symmetrically with trailing 8s if odd remainder.

Component: arc2_transform(layout_stack, Grid, Out)
  Purpose: Orchestrate corner detection, interior extraction, band/stretch
    finding, rotation, and output stacking.
  Decision: col_major path rotates blocks 90 CCW; row_major does not.
  Output: Stacked block rows concatenated into the output grid.

Score: 46/120 = 38.33% -> 47/120 = 39.17%.
Acc_347. SPARC: Specification v279, Pseudocode v271, Architecture v272,
  Refinement v331, Completion v333.

Component: arc2_fa_frame_colors_(Grid, Bg, FrameColors)
  Purpose: Identify which colors form the frame template.
  Strategy: Count cells per non-BG color; frame colors have count*2 >= max.
  Output: FrameColors list (1 color for clear winner, 2+ for ties).

Component: arc2_fa_frame_bbox_(Grid, FrameColors, R1, R2, C1, C2)
  Purpose: Compute bounding box of all frame-colored cells in the grid.
  Strategy: findall R-C for cells with frame color; min/max list.
  Output: Six integers defining the bbox.

Component: arc2_fa_holes_(Grid, Bg, R1, R2, C1, C2, Holes)
  Purpose: Collect BG cells inside the frame bbox.
  Strategy: between/3 scan; nth0 lookup.
  Output: Holes = list of absolute R-C pairs.

Component: arc2_fa_piece_comps_(Grid, Bg, FrameColors, PieceComps)
  Purpose: Find all non-BG 4-connected components that are not frame-colored.
  Strategy: arc2_jf_pieces_ then include/3 to exclude frame components.
  Output: PieceComps = list of R-C-V triple lists.

Component: arc2_fa_placements_(Norm, Holes, R1, C1, TR, TC, Placements)
  Purpose: Find absolute placement offsets where all piece cells land on holes.
  Strategy: Enumerate (DR0, DC0) in bbox; translate to absolute; forall check.
  Output: Placements = list of R0-C0 absolute top-left positions.

Component: arc2_fa_cover_(PiecesWP, RemHoles, Map0, Map)
  Purpose: Backtracking exact cover; assign each piece to a placement.
  Strategy: member/2 over Placements; re-validate against RemHoles; subtract.
  Output: Map = color map of (R-C)-V pairs for all hole positions.

Component: arc2_fa_build_(Grid, R1, R2, C1, C2, ColorMap, Out)
  Purpose: Extract output subgrid; fill holes from ColorMap.
  Strategy: numlist over RowIs, ColIs; memberchk lookup per cell.
  Output: Out = list-of-lists subgrid.

Component: arc2_transform(frame_assemble, Grid, Out)
  Purpose: Orchestrate frame detection, piece extraction, cover, and output.
  Decision: Reuses arc2_jf_mode_, arc2_jf_pieces_, arc2_jf_normalize_,
    arc2_jf_place_ from jigsaw_fill; frame_assemble adds 7 new fa_ helpers.
  Output: Subgrid = frame bbox with piece colors placed in all BG holes.

Score: 47/120 = 39.17% -> 48/120 = 40.00%.
Acc_348. SPARC: Specification v280, Pseudocode v272, Architecture v273,
  Refinement v332, Completion v338.

Component: arc2_qt_subgrid_(Grid, R0, R1, C0, C1, Sub)
  Purpose: Extract a rectangular subgrid between row/col index ranges.
  Strategy: numlist row/col; nth0 lookup per cell.
  Output: Sub = list-of-lists subgrid.

Component: arc2_qt_count_nz_(Grid, R0, R1, C0, C1, Count)
  Purpose: Count non-zero cells in a rectangular region.
  Strategy: findall 1 where V != 0; length of result.
  Output: Count = integer.

Component: arc2_qt_cell_(BR, BL, BRh, BRw, BLh, BLw, R, C, V)
  Purpose: Compute output value at (R,C) using tile and fill rules.
  Strategy: tile_r=R mod BRh, tile_c=C mod BRw, ti=R div BRh;
    if BR[tile_r][tile_c] != 0 use it; else use BL[ti mod BLh][tile_c mod BLw].
  Output: V = cell value.

Component: arc2_transform(quadrant_tile, Grid, Out)
  Purpose: Orchestrate quadrant split, dimension counting, tile-and-fill.
  Decision: SplitR=R//2, SplitC=C//2 divides all task inputs correctly.
  Output: Out = TLCount x TRCount grid.

Wave 52 - plus_mark (WP-310, Layer 285):
  Component: arc2_pm_is_plus_center_(Grid, H, W, R, C)
    Input: Grid (list-of-lists), H (rows), W (cols), R and C (candidate center).
    Output: succeeds when all 5 plus-shape cells hold value 4.
    Uses nth0 lookups for center row and the two neighbor rows.
  Component: arc2_pm_plus_cells_(Grid, H, W, PlusCells)
    Input: Grid, H, W.
    Output: PlusCells - sorted list of R-C pairs for all cells in any plus-shape.
    Uses between/3 to enumerate all candidate centers; findall collects the
    center and 4 neighbors for each valid center; sort removes duplicates.
  Component: arc2_transform(plus_mark, Grid, Out)
    Input: Grid.
    Output: Out - grid with plus-shape cells set to 8.
    Uses maplist over row and column index lists; memberchk against PlusCells
    selects 8 vs the original cell value.

Wave 53 - template_expand (WP-311, Layer 286):

Components:

1. arc2_te_bg_(Grid, BG):
   Flatten all cells, msort, scan for mode value. O(H*W*log(H*W)).

2. arc2_te_mode_(SortedList, Mode) / arc2_te_mode_scan_(Rest, Cur, N, BestV, BestN, Mode):
   Linear scan over sorted list tracking current run and best run.

3. arc2_te_isolated_(Grid, BG, H, W, R, C):
   Checks cell (R,C) is non-BG and none of its 4 orthogonal neighbours
   within bounds is non-BG. Used by arc2_te_templ_cells_.

4. arc2_te_templ_cells_(Grid, BG, H, W, TemplCells):
   findall over all positions, filter by arc2_te_isolated_. Returns R-C pairs.

5. arc2_te_col_runs_(SortedCols, Runs) / arc2_te_col_runs_scan_:
   Partitions a sorted integer list into maximal contiguous runs S-E.

6. arc2_te_seed_info_(Grid, BG, H, W, TemplCells, SeedRowMin, ColRuns,
                       BH, BW, Stride, SeedColors):
   Finds all non-BG non-template cells, computes row extent, col runs,
   block dimensions, stride, and colors per sub-block.

7. arc2_te_template_structure_(TemplCells, TRows, TCols):
   Extracts sorted lists of distinct template rows and columns.

8. arc2_te_check_match_(Grid, TRows, TCols, SeedColors, LI, C0, I):
   Recursive check: template[TRows[LI]][TCols[C0+I]] == SeedColors[I].

9. arc2_te_find_level_(Grid, TRows, TCols, SeedColors, SeedLevel, CGOff):
   Double between/3 search over (level, col-group offset) pairs; commits
   on first consistent match via cut.

10. arc2_te_in_block_(X, Anchor, Stride, BlockSize, NumBlocks, BIdx):
    Succeeds when X falls inside block BIdx of a regular tiling:
    DX=X-Anchor >= 0; BIdx=DX//Stride < NumBlocks; DX-BIdx*Stride < BlockSize.

11. arc2_transform(template_expand, Grid, Out):
    Top-level predicate: calls steps 1-10, then maplist over rows/cols to
    build Out. Each cell queries arc2_te_in_block_ for both row and col to
    determine block indices, reads template color, emits it or copies input.

Data flow:
  Grid -> bg_ -> templ_cells_ -> seed_info_ -> template_structure_
       -> find_level_ -> AnchorRow/AnchorCol -> maplist -> Out

noise_erase (Layer 287, WP-312):
arc2_ne_1nbr_count_/4: counts in-bounds 4-neighbors with value 1 using include/3
  and arc2_cell_/4.
arc2_ne_avail_count_/4: counts total in-bounds 4-neighbors using arc2_cell_/4 to
  test bounds implicitly.
arc2_ne_stray0_seed_/3: combines 1nbr_count and avail_count with min(3,avail)
  threshold to detect stray-0 seeds.
arc2_ne_stray1_/3: detects 1-cells with <=1 same-valued neighbor.
arc2_ne_expand_bfs_/4: iterative BFS queue expansion; deduplicates each wave
  with sort/2; appends new cells to both visited list and queue tail.
arc2_ne_stray0_all_/4: findall seeds then calls expand_bfs_ from the sorted
  seed set to produce the complete stray-0 list.
arc2_ne_frame_/3: findall 8-neighbor positions of all stray-0 cells; deduplicates
  with sort/2; excludes positions already in stray-0.
arc2_ne_out_val_/7: priority if-then-else: stray-0 -> 0; frame -> 7;
  stray-1 -> 0; else arc2_cell_ copy.
arc2_transform(noise_erase)/3: orchestrates all above predicates then builds
  output via maplist over row/col index lists.

pocket_shot (Layer 288, WP-313):
arc2_ps_dr_/2, arc2_ps_dc_/2: lookup tables for row/col delta per direction.
arc2_ps_perpdirs_/2: lookup table for the two perpendicular directions per axis.
arc2_ps_opp_/2: opposite direction lookup.
arc2_ps_scan_/6: scans in direction D from (R,C), skipping BG/2 cells, until
  a non-BG non-2 arm-cell is found; uses arc2_ps_scan_go_/7 recursively.
arc2_ps_scan_go_/7: base case returns R-C when arm-cell found; step case
  advances one cell and recurses; fails at grid boundary.
arc2_ps_valid_peg_/4: three-condition interior peg check: (1) opposite-direction
  neighbor is BG/off-grid; (2) parent arm-cell exists in D; (3) parent has >=2
  arm-cell neighbors in perpendicular directions (uses include/3).
arc2_ps_arm_nbr_/4: helper for valid_peg_; succeeds if PD-direction neighbor
  of (R,C) is a non-BG non-2 cell.
arc2_ps_peg_col_/6: combines scan_ and valid_peg_ for vertical firing (per col).
arc2_ps_peg_row_/6: combines scan_ and valid_peg_ for horizontal firing (per row).
arc2_ps_vland_/4, arc2_ps_hland_/4: compute landing bounding box given the
  common arm row/col (XAR or XAC); four clauses cover up/down/left/right.
arc2_ps_fire_/5: tries all four directions via member/2; for each direction uses
  maplist with peg_col_ or peg_row_; sort(XRs,[XAR]) enforces block integrity;
  calls vland_/hland_ to get landing box.
arc2_ps_find_blocks_/2: findall of 2-cells, sort, then arc2_ps_comps_/4.
arc2_ps_comps_/4: iterates sorted 2-cells; skips already-seen cells; BFS-expands
  via arc2_bfs_/7 to collect component; min/max-list computes bounding box.
arc2_ps_trail_/5: four direction clauses compute Twos (landing cells) and Zeros
  (original block + trail cells) via findall + between.
arc2_ps_solve_/6, arc2_ps_solve_acc_/9: iterate blocks; once(arc2_ps_fire_) to
  determine fate; append to Zeros/Twos or Erases; final sort deduplicates.
arc2_ps_out_/8: priority if-then-else: TwoSet -> 2; ZeroSet -> 0;
  EraseSet -> BG; else arc2_cell_ copy.
arc2_transform(pocket_shot)/3: bg_, find_blocks_, solve_, maplist output.
arc2_induce_rule(pocket_shot): fast specific clause with 2-cell pre-filter placed
  before the generic catch-all to avoid timeout on large grids.

shape_walk (Layer 289, WP-314):
arc2_sw_divider_col_/2: scans columns left to right; first column where
  forall(member(Row, Grid), nth0(DC, Row, 4)) holds is the divider. Uses cut
  after first success for efficiency.
arc2_sw_five_rc_/3: scans all (R,C) positions via between/3; succeeds at first
  cell with value 5 via arc2_cell_/4 and cut.
arc2_sw_nonblank_rows_/3: findall over rows 0..H-1; keeps row R if once/1 finds
  any column C in 0..DC-1 with non-zero value (via nth0/3).
arc2_sw_section_starts_/2: recursive list traversal; for each head R, uses
  select/3 twice to consume R+1 and R+2 from the tail (enforcing consecutive
  triples); the result list contains only the first row of each section.
arc2_sw_block_color_/4: enumerates the nine (Ri,Ci) pairs for the 3x3 block;
  once/1 returns the first non-zero value found via arc2_cell_/4.
arc2_sw_norm_/2: two clauses; first clause catches 0 and returns 0; second
  clause catches any non-zero and returns 1. Used inside maplist/3 to normalize
  all nine cells of a block.
arc2_sw_block_shape_/4: reads all nine cells via arc2_cell_/4; calls maplist
  with arc2_sw_norm_ to produce N00..N22; assembles Shape = [[R0],[R1],[R2]].
arc2_sw_shape_to_move_/3: four deterministic clauses with cut; each clause
  unifies the normalized shape and returns direction atom and integer length.
arc2_sw_seg_cells_/5: three clauses (left, right, down); uses findall with
  between/3 to generate cell positions; LEFT generates Cend..C, RIGHT generates
  C..Cend, DOWN generates R..Rend.
arc2_sw_seg_tip_/5: three clauses compute the last cell coordinates: LEFT tip
  col = C-Len+1, RIGHT tip col = C+Len-1, DOWN tip row = R+Len-1.
arc2_sw_walk_/5: recursive; base case empty list. Step case: call seg_cells_ to
  get positions, seg_tip_ to get tip, compute NR=TipR+1; recurse on remaining
  blocks; findall tags each position with color; append merges current segment
  with recursive result.
arc2_sw_blocks_at_/4: findall over SectStarts; for each section start SR,
  calls block_color_, block_shape_, shape_to_move_ to build blk/3 term.
arc2_transform(shape_walk)/3: top-level orchestrator; calls divider_col_,
  five_rc_, nonblank_rows_, section_starts_, blocks_at_ twice (left and mid),
  append, walk_, then maplist over row/col indices to build H x DC output.
  Output cell priority: row-0 5-marker > chain cells (member/3 first match) > 0.
arc2_induce_rule(shape_walk): fast specific clause placed before catch-all;
  pre-filter checks that first row of first training input contains both a 5
  and a 4; full verification via forall + arc2_transform.

Layer 290 frame_reflect Architecture (WP-315):
arc2_fr_frame_/3: row-major scan for first non-8 cell = frame top-left.
arc2_fr_sub3_/4: read 9 cells at offsets from (SR,SC) into 3x3 matrix.
arc2_fr_rot180_/2: single fact reversing both element and row order.
arc2_fr_mix_/6: four-clause arm-product selector: both->Filler; left->AI; top->AI; neither->Corner.
arc2_fr_hole_fill_/6: reads arms + corners; applies mix to 9 positions; returns R-C-V list.
arc2_transform(frame_reflect)/3: frame_+findall(8 stamps)+hole_fill_+maplist.

Layer 291 cross_reflect Architecture (WP-316):
arc2_cr_cross_/4: scan rows for one where sort=[V]!=BG; then scan cols for col
  where all cells = same V; two cuts stop at first match.
arc2_cr_bbox_q_/10: findall Row-Col in quadrant RLo..RHi x CLo..CHi with value V;
  extract Rs and Cs; min_list/max_list for tight bounding box.
arc2_cr_anchor_/5: scan TR quadrant in row-major order; first non-BG cell value
  is the anchor; cut stops immediately.
arc2_cr_sats_/6: findall non-BG non-anchor values in TL (rows<R, cols<C); sort
  deduplicates to one entry per satellite colour.
arc2_cr_sat_info_/7: calls bbox_q_ in TL for satellite value SV; computes
  DR=MinR-AR, DC=MinC-AC, SH=height, SW=width.
arc2_cr_mods_(tr)/11: LR-reflect: NewDC=N_tl-DC-SW; scale all dims by N_q//N_tl;
  placed block corners MinR/MaxR/MinC/MaxC; findall R-C-SV.
arc2_cr_mods_(br)/11: 180-rotate: NewDR=N_tl-DR-SH and NewDC=N_tl-DC-SW; scale;
  findall R-C-SV.
arc2_cr_mods_(bl)/11: TB-reflect: NewDR=N_tl-DR-SH; DC unchanged; scale;
  findall R-C-SV.
arc2_transform(cross_reflect)/3: cross_ + anchor_ + sats_ + maplist(sat_info_) +
  bbox_q_ x3 for TR/BR/BL + findall(mods_) x3 + append x3 + maplist output.
arc2_induce_rule(cross_reflect): pre-filter checks arc2_cr_cross_ on first
  training input; full forall verification.

Layer 292 - WP-317 - scaled_frame architecture

arc2_sf_frame_/6: iterates distinct non-0 colors; for each builds bounding box
  of all same-color cells; checks R1>R0+1, C1>C0+1; calls arc2_sf_solid_border_;
  requires at least one 0-cell in interior; cuts on first success.
arc2_sf_solid_border_/6: forall over top/bottom rows checks every col = FC;
  forall over all rows checks left and right cols = FC.
arc2_sf_holes_/6: findall over interior (rows R0+1..R1-1, cols C0+1..C1-1)
  where grid value = 0.
arc2_sf_objects_/7: findall non-0 non-FC cells outside frame bbox; extracts
  R-C positions; calls arc2_sf_conn_comps_; include size >= 4; maps to V-Comp.
arc2_sf_scale_/2: maplist lengths; arc2_sf_gcd_list_ (folding gcd/2); round(sqrt).
arc2_sf_gcd_list_/2: base case single element; recursive fold using gcd/2.
arc2_sf_conn_comps_/2: sort to dedup; calls arc2_sf_comps_.
arc2_sf_comps_/2: base []; recursive: take Seed, BFS, recurse on Remaining.
arc2_sf_bfs_/5: base case [] queue; per step: compute 4-neighbors; findall
  neighbors in Avail not in Visited; subtract from Avail; append to Visited
  and Queue; recurse.
arc2_sf_match_/4: maplist annotate HComps with (len,centcol,HC); maplist annotate
  Objects with (len//Scale2,centcol,V); msort both; maplist arc2_sf_pair_match_.
arc2_sf_centcol_/2: findall cols; sumlist + length -> mean.
arc2_sf_cell_val_/8: FRow=FR0+R//Scale; FCol=FC0+C//Scale; read GVal; if 0
  call arc2_sf_hole_color_; else Val=FC.
arc2_sf_hole_color_/4: member search over Matches for HComp containing R-C.
arc2_transform(scaled_frame)/3: delegates to arc2_sf_solve_.
arc2_induce_rule(scaled_frame): pre-filter arc2_sf_frame_ on first pair;
  forall training pairs verify arc2_transform(scaled_frame).

Layer 293 - WP-318 - layout_tile architecture
arc2_lt_solve_/2: top-level: dividers -> groups -> subgrids -> assignments -> output.

arc2_lt_divider_cols_/2: findall cols where all {0,5} and contains at least one 5.
arc2_lt_row_groups_/5: split into 3 contiguous content row-groups.
arc2_lt_col_groups_/3: split into N contiguous content col-groups.
arc2_lt_contiguous_groups_/2: split sorted index list into maximal runs.
arc2_lt_subgrid_/4: extract subgrid by row/col index lists.

arc2_lt_assignments_/3: (br,bc,TI) for each layout non-zero non-5 cell.
arc2_lt_build_output_/5: S^2 x S^2 output via nested findall.
