WP 397-400: The ARC-AGI-3 Readiness Suite (co_*, Layers 372-375) release note (2026-07-10)
New packs: packs/curiosity, packs/goal_inference, packs/efficiency_governor,
  packs/arc3_protocol — 12 files, 41 public predicates, 27 PLUnit tests, all
  green, loading cleanly alongside the six-pack Causalontology suite.
Rationale: comprehensive research into the ARC-AGI-3 Interactive Reasoning
  Benchmark (ARC Prize Foundation; launched 25 March 2026; frontier models
  under one percent, humans one hundred percent) found the arc3_harness harness
  supplies the perceive-learn-plan-act loop but leaves four benchmark-defining
  capabilities to the caller. This suite closes them. curiosity is the
  exploration policy the two strongest developer-preview agents converged on:
  a canonical order-free state signature that recognises a returned-to state
  as a loop, a preference for actions the causal graph predicts will change
  the frame over dead ones, curiosity by least-tried, hazards never chosen,
  and salient click targeting that reduces the ACTION6 cell-select from four
  thousand cells to the objects' centroids. goal_inference infers the unstated
  win condition by accumulating support for the frame-change features that
  precede a reported WIN and discounting those that also precede a loss,
  exposing the hypothesis as both an abstract goal and a changed/4 occurrent
  the planner can aim at, with a confidence reading. efficiency_governor is the
  efficiency governor for the RHAE-style scoring the benchmark rewards: it
  counts actions per level, holds the human baseline, caps spending at five
  times the human, and computes the per-level score min(1,H/A) squared, the
  weighted environment score, and the total percentage. arc3_protocol pins the
  exact March-2026 protocol vocabulary as inspectable facts — the ACTION1
  through ACTION7 and RESET commands under /api/cmd, the cell-select ACTION6
  with x and y, scorecard open and close, the four game states with WIN and
  GAME_OVER terminal, sixty-four-cell frames of colours zero to fifteen — and
  a guarded arc3_protocol_env adapter packaging the live protocol as a arc3_harness
  environment.
Companion: the Mentova side adds an autonomous ARC-AGI-3 agent driver that
  wires this suite into the game body, and the preparation dossier
  docs/ARC-AGI-3_Preparation_v1.txt. No benchmark score is claimed: the
  result remains a labelled and falsifiable bet, to be reported only once
  measured against the live leaderboard.
SPARC: Specification v355, Pseudocode v347, Architecture v348, Refinement v407, Completion v413.

WP 401: The ARC-AGI-3 Human-Step Ladder in J-Space (human_steps, Layer 376) release note (2026-07-10)
New pack: packs/human_steps - 3 files, 15 public predicates, 8 PLUnit tests,
  all green, loading cleanly beside the Causalontology and ARC-AGI-3 Readiness
  suites and the jspace concept workspace.
Rationale: comprehensive research into how humans actually play ARC-AGI-3
  (the ARC Prize human study - 458 participants, in-person, first-run, one
  attempt each) confirmed the explore-then-execute shape of play and, with the
  merged Human Steps deconstruction, its full six-phase, thirty-micro-step
  ladder: orient to the frame; probe the controls and build a world model;
  infer the unstated goal; plan an efficient route; execute while monitoring;
  and carry knowledge forward across levels. human_steps encodes that ladder as
  ordered facts (human_steps_phase, human_steps_step, human_steps_ladder, human_steps_phase_capability) and holds
  the step the agent is currently on as a concept in a J-Space workspace (the
  jspace pack - the Jacobian Space, read through the Jacobian Lens), so the
  J-Lens readout says which human step the agent is executing and walking the
  ladder leaves a glass-box trace of the whole process. The pack also makes
  the probe phase concrete with the discrete action-response Jacobian:
  human_steps_sensitivity (change per action), human_steps_controllable (the object the agent
  controls, being the colour whose centroid moves most), human_steps_jacobian (that
  object's per-action displacement - the partial derivatives of its position),
  and human_steps_goal_gradient (actions ranked toward a goal cell - the gradient the
  execution phase descends).
Companion: the Mentova side adds a human-step solo controller that walks this
  ladder over a navigation game, keeping the process live in the J-Lens as
  Mentova attempts ARC-AGI-3 environments unaided, and the dossier
  docs/ARC-AGI-3_Human_Steps_v1.txt recording the full ladder in the J-Space
  framing. No benchmark score is claimed.
SPARC: Specification v356, Pseudocode v348, Architecture v349, Refinement v408, Completion v414.

WP 402: Causalontology State-Graph Exploration (state_graph, Layer 377) release note (2026-07-10)
New pack: packs/state_graph - 3 files, 11 public predicates, 6 PLUnit tests, all
  green, no dependencies.
Rationale: deep research into ARC-AGI-3 solving techniques (the graph-based
  exploration paper, arXiv 2512.24156, third on the public leaderboard; the
  developer-preview winners; the ARC Prize 2026 Milestone 1 writeups) found that
  the agents which score are not the frontier language models - which score
  under one percent - but agents that keep a directed graph of the states they
  have seen and the actions they have tried, and always move toward the nearest
  unexplored frontier. That technique solved a median of thirty levels across
  six games where the language-plus-DSL baseline solved five. state_graph is that
  technique as glass-box PrologAI: nodes are frame hashes; edges are observed
  state-to-action-to-next-state transitions; each tried pair is marked tested and
  each no-change action dead; and state_graph_choose implements the winning hierarchical
  rule - probe an untested non-dead action in the current state, else take the
  first step on the shortest breadth-first path to the nearest state with an
  untested action, else fail so the caller falls back. The graph persists across
  attempts for carry-forward.
Companion: the Mentova side wires state_graph into the live solo player (the chat
  backend's action choice consults the graph before least-tried curiosity) and
  records the solving-techniques findings in docs/ARC-AGI-3_Preparation_v1.txt.
  No benchmark score is claimed.
SPARC: Specification v357, Pseudocode v349, Architecture v350, Refinement v409, Completion v415.

================================================================================
APPENDED SECTION — THE COGNITIVE COMPLETION SUITE (WP-409 through WP-416)
================================================================================

Architecture. The eight packs are self-contained (requires([])) and layer cleanly above the existing co_ family: safety_governor mirrors in causal_core's preventive relations without a hard dependency; attention can consume a novelty signal from world_model and an affect signal from affect; motivation feeds goals to causal_planner and goal_inference; episodic_memory and consolidation sit beside causal_core as the experiential and housekeeping memory. The dependency graph stays acyclic.

The eight packs, at Layers 384 through 391, each self-contained, glass-box,
ERC-commented, and PLUnit-tested, and each renamed away from the source concept
names in THE_BUILDING_FILES while preserving the idea and the Causalontology
Architecture Standard (CAS):

  episodic_memory    (WP-409, Layer 384) episodic memory — reified experience-cases
              recalled by feature overlap, replayed, and reinforced.
  attention (WP-410, Layer 385) attention and broadcast — score by novelty,
              relevance, and affect; a bounded working set; one broadcast winner.
  motivation  (WP-411, Layer 386) motivation — homeostatic set-points whose gap
              becomes pressure, and a never-empty prioritized goal agenda.
  affect   (WP-412, Layer 387) affect — appraise events into valence and
              arousal, hold a running temperament, pre-flavor options, expose coping.
  metacognition    (WP-413, Layer 388) metacognition — per-strategy calibration,
              confusion detection, progress trend, keep/switch/seek-guidance.
  safety_governor     (WP-414, Layer 389) safety governor — an immutable constitution,
              a pre-action veto with a reason, and an append-only veto log.
  repair     (WP-415, Layer 390) repair — inversion, then neutralization, then
              re-route, then accept, the Piagetian equilibration move as rules.
  consolidation  (WP-416, Layer 391) consolidation — merge duplicates, compress a
              reliable sequence into one composite, forget stale low-value records.

QA of the prior eighteen co_ packs found all green; the only real defect,
missing ERC comments in packs/object_relations/pack.pl, was fixed in the same change. All
twenty-six co_ packs pass their suites on the full cross-pack library path.

Architecture. All four packs are self-contained (requires([])) and compose with the family: grounding emits terms the noun_backbone / causal_core / causal_planner layers consume (continuant, disposition, goal, preventive); theory_of_mind complements goal_inference by modelling OTHER agents' goals rather than the environment's; analogy operates on the rel(Type,A,B) output of object_relations; and concept_formation's induced concepts suggest is-a candidates for the noun_backbone backbone. The four packs, at Layers 392 through 395, each self-contained, glass-box,
ERC-commented, and PLUnit-tested, and each renamed away from the source concept
names in THE_BUILDING_FILES while preserving the idea and the CAS:

  grounding (WP-417, Layer 392) clue/language grounding — the grounding seam of
            Causalontology_v5 Section 10: a human clue plus a referent becomes a
            list of Causalontology assertions (continuant, disposition, goal, or
            preventive), tagged as a high-confidence but defeasible human hint.
  theory_of_mind    (WP-418, Layer 393) theory of mind — infer another agent's goal from
            the targets its moves approach, predict its next step, and name a
            false belief the true state contradicts (Sally-Anne).

            sets: the injective object mapping that preserves the most relations,
            with transfer of a known rule across the mapping.
  concept_formation  (WP-420, Layer 395) concept formation — induce categories by seed
            clustering of feature bundles, coin concept(Id,Core,Members), and
            classify a new item whose features contain the core.

These close the two honestly-named gaps of the Cognitive Completion wave (a
co_-native social cognition and a co_-native language grounding) and add two
core inference faculties THE_BUILDING_FILES emphasise — analogy and concept
formation. All thirty co_ packs pass on the full cross-pack library path.

Architecture. All four packs are self-contained (requires([])) and compose with the family: imagination extends world_model's in-model rollout with reality partitioning and a promotion discipline; priming complements attention (priming decides what becomes relevant, salience picks the one winner); regulation refines individual behaviours below causal_learning and metacognition; lore sits above episodic_memory, abstracting episodes into advice. The four packs, at Layers 396 through 399, each self-contained, glass-box,
ERC-commented, PLUnit-tested, and renamed away from the source concept names in
THE_BUILDING_FILES while preserving the idea and the CAS:

  imagination   (WP-421, Layer 396) imagination — roll a start state forward through
            a transition model into a quarantined "imagined" reality (one of
            observed/desired/expected/imagined/recalled), score whether it reaches
            a goal, pick the fewest-step plan, and cross into fact only by a
            deliberate promotion.
  priming  (WP-422, Layer 397) priming — spreading activation over a weighted
            association graph by widest-path relaxation with per-hop decay; the
            complement to attention (what becomes relevant vs which one wins).
  regulation   (WP-423, Layer 398) regulation — classify feedback into the four
            flavours (confirming, disappointing, serendipitous, shocking) and,
            when a behaviour both wins and loses, find the discriminating feature
            and refine the rule to require or shun it.
  lore   (WP-424, Layer 399) lore — detect recurring themes, recall the
            lessons of matching past situations, and distil a maxim (do the
            response that usually works, else avoid the worst).

Architecture. world_model becomes the single two-mode world model; nexus and the Mentova AGI-Foundations demo now depend on world_model rather than worldmodel; the dependency graph stays acyclic and one name collision is removed.

The unification program treats PrologAI as the cognitive architecture and
Causalontology as the data-structure language every part should speak, with the
Lattice / APEX_MIND nexus as the one shared store. Its convergence pattern is
absorb-and-supersede: merge a redundant older pack into the canonical co_ pack
(the union of both, plus Causalontology structure), union the test suites,
migrate all callers across both repositories, verify zero references, then delete
the older pack (clean delete, no shim - a private pre-release system). The first
convergence merged the structured worldmodel pack (WP-385) into world_model, now a
single two-mode world model: MODE 1 the learned transition tallies (predict /
verify / repair / rollout / laws) and MODE 2 the STRIPS simulate-and-plan model
(states, actions, simulate, breadth-first plan, reachability, enumerate, learn),
plus a world_model_as_cros/2 bridge that emits the learned model as reified CROs. The two
colliding names were reconciled (worldmodel world_model_predict/4 -> world_model_model_predict/4;
world_model_rollout/4 -> world_model_enumerate/4), resolving a real platform-wide name collision.
world_model's suite is the union: 30 tests, all green; all 34 co_ packs plus nexus
pass; worldmodel deleted with zero live references remaining. Renames and
deletions are tracked in output/co_Convergence_Ledger_1.txt.

NAMING CONVENTION - MEGA MERGE WAVE FOUR FINAL (co_plan renamed; planner kept separate; the co_ prefix is fully retired)

The last co_ pack. A Section E style keep-or-merge decision was made and recorded: the naming table had co_plan absorb the planner pack and take the name planner. That merge was declined. co_plan is a backward causal-chain planner over the Causalontology Causal Relation Object graph (it composes procedures as sequence-cause relations and searches the causal graph backward from a goal, respecting the learned avoid-set); the planner pack is a Hierarchical Task Network engine (WP-386) - one of the seven flagship AGI-Foundations packs, wired through the nexus - that decomposes compound tasks through named methods into primitive actions over sorted-fluent states. These are different planning paradigms over different data models, not one redundant faculty. Folding the flagship HTN foundation into the small causal planner would bury it, exactly as actinf was kept out of affect and sentinels out of verification. So planner is KEPT SEPARATE and untouched, and co_plan takes a standalone whole-word name that does not collide: causal_planner, with pack-qualified predicates (co_plan to causal_planner_plan, co_plan_chain to causal_planner_chain, co_compose_procedure, co_procedure, co_achievable, co_plan_safe, co_execute). Callers migrated across both repositories: arc3_harness, hierarchical_planning, human_steps, and repair here, and the two Mentova ARC modules in the companion change.

THE co_ PREFIX IS NOW FULLY RETIRED. All thirty-four original co_ packs have been converted to whole-word snake_case names with pack-qualified predicates. Causalontology is the architecture, not a subset marked by a prefix.

SPARC: Specification v376, Pseudocode v368, Architecture v369, Refinement v428, Completion v434.

NAMING CONVENTION - MEGA MERGE WAVE FOUR POST-MERGE AUDIT HOTFIX

A six-dimension independent audit of the completed co_ retirement found the full library green (two hundred sixty-two of two hundred sixty-two pack test files pass, zero co_ directories, all documentation and git and PR and CI state clean) but surfaced three real defects introduced by the merges, now fixed:

One, the curiosity pack manifest wrongly listed node_facts in requires. node_facts is not a pack; it is a module inside the lattice pack, and no other pack lists it. The absorbed intrinsic-motivation half uses library(node_facts) ambiently over the library path, exactly as ten other packs do without a requires entry. The manifest is corrected to requires([causal_core, causal_learning, grid, gridobj]), matching the exploration half's original dependencies. Curiosity's twelve tests still pass.

Two and three, in the Mentova repository, two file_search_path strings still pointed at directories deleted by the merges: the AGI-foundations demo pointed at packs/tom/prolog (the tom pack was absorbed into theory_of_mind) while calling library(theory_of_mind), and the attention-schema wrapper pointed at packs/attention_schema/prolog (absorbed into attention) while calling library(attention). Because these files register their own search path inside a load-time initialization directive, they resolved under an external test path but would fail to self-load in production. Both are corrected to the surviving pack directories and verified by a standalone consult with no external path. The lesson: when a pack directory is renamed, sweep callers for hardcoded packs/OLD/prolog path strings, not only use_module and predicate names.

SPARC: Specification v377, Pseudocode v369, Architecture v370, Refinement v429, Completion v435.

PACK MANIFEST HYGIENE - sentinels requires corrected

The sentinels pack manifest declared requires(prologai_expand), a dependency on something that is not a pack: prologai_expand is a module living at syntax/prolog/prologai_expand.pl, and syntax is not a pack, so nothing declares provides(prologai_expand). The declaration was also written as a bare atom rather than the conventional list. The sentinels module imports nothing at all (it is a pure provider of pai_register_sentinel and sentinel_retract, used by the reflection pack), so the dependency was vestigial, dating to the PR-9 bootstrap. The manifest is corrected to requires([]), the standard form for a pack that needs only the standard library. Sentinels still loads, and the reflection pack that imports it still loads. This defect was pre-existing and unrelated to the co_ retirement; it was surfaced by that program's post-merge audit and fixed here for hygiene.

SPARC: Specification v378, Pseudocode v370, Architecture v371, Refinement v430, Completion v436.

TEST HARNESS STANDARDIZATION - dreaming onto PLUnit

The dreaming pack shipped a bespoke test harness: seven test_* predicates driven by a hand-written run_tests/0 under a :- initialization(run_tests, main) directive. Because the file defined its own run_tests/0, the standard PLUnit invocation (swipl -g "run_tests, halt") reported No tests to run, so the suite was invisible to the standard runner even though its seven acceptance tests passed when run directly. The suite is now converted to PLUnit begin_tests(dreaming)/test()/end_tests blocks with assertion/1 checks, with no change to what is tested (the same seven acceptance criteria AC-PR52-001 through AC-PR52-007 over pai_dream_record, pai_dream_journal, pai_dream_generative_replay, pai_dream_slow_wave, pai_dream_rem, pai_dream_counterfactual, and pai_dream_cycle). All seven now pass under the standard run_tests invocation. This completes the PLUnit standardization begun for the six earlier bespoke-harness suites; dreaming was the last, missed because it is a kept-separate infrastructure pack outside the co_ family. The pai_dream_ predicate names are unchanged: dreaming was deliberately kept separate from the imagination convergence and retains its own prefix.

SPARC: Specification v379, Pseudocode v371, Architecture v372, Refinement v431, Completion v437.

NAMING CONVENTION - dreaming predicates made pack-qualified

The dreaming pack was deliberately kept separate from the imagination convergence (it is the Lattice-integrated dream engine), but the naming convention still applies to it: predicate names must be pack-qualified whole-word snake_case. Its predicates carried the legacy pai_dream_ prefix on the seven exports (pai_dream_cycle, pai_dream_record, pai_dream_journal, pai_dream_generative_replay, pai_dream_slow_wave, pai_dream_rem, pai_dream_counterfactual) and a bare dream_ prefix on eleven internal helpers. The dream_report/5 output term and the dream/2 identifier are DATA-structure functors, not predicates, and are preserved unchanged - the convention governs predicate names, not the data vocabulary a pack emits. The pack had no external callers; only its own PLUnit test needed updating, and its seven tests pass. Kept-separate does not mean exempt from the naming convention, only exempt from the merge.

PROJECT DE-JAMMING — DATA LAYER: RULE, LINTER, AND WAVE E1

The de-jamming rule is made universal and permanent (CLAUDE.md NAMING CONVENTION RULE clauses four and five): every predicate in every pack, new or existing, must be prefixed with the pack's full whole-word name; terse two-letter and abbreviated prefixes are banned outright, because they collide across packs (wm meant both world-model and wallpaper-motif; lk_ means both link and lookup) and are opaque to newcomers. A new pack must ship pack-qualified from its first commit. Enforcement is a script, bin/check_pack_naming.sh, that flags any pack whose predicate prefix is not its own name and reports shared prefixes; it is a merge blocker for a new or renamed pack. The standing Data-Layer De-Jamming Program (output/DeJam_Data_Layer_Plan.txt) brings the two hundred forty-seven legacy Data-Layer packs still on terse prefixes into line, in waves - the one hundred seventy-eight exclusive-prefix packs batched first, then the sixty-nine collision-prefix packs handled individually so each takes its own whole-word predicates and the shared stub dissolves.

Wave E1 (exclusive, zero-caller leaf packs): arith ar_ to arith_, assemble as_ to assemble_, autom at_ to autom_, block bk_ to block_, border br_ to border_, bound bd_ to bound_, canvas cv_ to canvas_, cellset cs_ to cellset_, colormap cm_ to colormap_, colortable ct_ to colortable_. About one hundred ninety predicates by exact-name substitution; every one of the ten verified to have no external caller in either repository first, so the change is confined to each pack's own module and test. All ten pass; the full library regresses at two hundred fifty-eight packs green; the linter reports zero violations for the ten.

It now reports zero violations across all packs. Two hundred fifty-eight packs green.

PROJECT DE-JAMMING — SWI STDLIB SHADOW GUARD

The naming linter gains a fourth merge-blocking check: a pack name may not shadow an SWI-Prolog standard-library module. The check queries the installed SWI library directory live, with a hardcoded core fallback, and flags any pack whose name equals a stdlib module. Beyond the arithmetic case already fixed, it surfaced two genuine shadows - sort (library(sort)) and table (library(table)) - renamed to sorting and data_table, their exclusive prefixes and callers migrated exact-name across both repositories. The tabling pack was inspected and left unchanged: its module file is lattice_tabling.pl, not tabling.pl, so library(tabling) correctly resolves to the SWI standard library and the pack does not shadow it. All packs load; two hundred fifty-eight green; the linter reports zero violations across all four checks.

SPARC: Specification v399, Pseudocode v391, Architecture v392, Refinement v451, Completion v457.

KEEP-SEPARATE BOUNDARY DOCUMENTED — reflection vs metacognition

The reflection pack's header now records why it is kept separate from the metacognition faculty, applying the convergence-review discipline that keeps a distinct or flagship faculty from being buried in a merge. reflection is the runtime actor/scheduler engine - twelve cyclic actors and two sentinels driving the live scheduler, importing cyclic_actor, the Lattice, node_facts, scopes, and sentinels - whereas metacognition is a pure self-monitor (per-strategy calibration, confusion detection) importing only lists. The two collaborate but sit at different abstraction layers, a faculty versus the engine that runs it. This mirrors the boundary the imagination pack already documents against the Lattice-integrated dreaming engine. Comment-only; no behaviour change; two hundred fifty-eight packs green.

SPARC: Specification v400, Pseudocode v392, Architecture v393, Refinement v452, Completion v458.

PACK RENAME — reflection to reflex_actors (clarity over provenance)

The reflection pack is renamed reflex_actors. As the convergence review noted, its NAME - reading as introspection or metacognition - was the one most likely to invite a wrong re-merge into the metacognition faculty, though the two are the furthest apart in implementation: reflex_actors is the runtime actor/scheduler engine (twelve cyclic actors and two sentinels reacting to internal conditions on the live scheduler), while metacognition is a pure self-monitor. The owner ruled clarity over provenance, so the pack, module, manifest, and its eighteen predicates take the whole-word name reflex_actors_ (reflex_actors_install_actors, and so on), the sole caller - the pr13 acceptance suite - is migrated, and the Reflection Pattern name survives in prose as the Section 3.11 provenance. reflex_actors loads clean; the linter is zero; two hundred fifty-eight packs green.

SPARC: Specification v404, Pseudocode v396, Architecture v397, Refinement v456, Completion v462.

REGRESSION HARDENING — FORTY PACKS GAIN IN-PACK TESTS, A ROTTED CRYPTO PACK FIXED

Forty packs had no in-pack test and were therefore not in the per-pack regression, so any rot in them was invisible - as the lattice_cryptography pack proved. It carried six self-recursive encrypt/decrypt stub clauses (head :- head) that overflowed the stack when called, and an export list declaring encrypt_ecdh/4 and encrypt_pqc/4 that only the stubs satisfied while the real implementations are the five-argument forms reached through the generic dispatch. The stubs are removed, the export arities corrected to /5, and the ECDH and post-quantum callers routed through the clean generic encrypt/5 and decrypt/5 interface. Every one of the forty packs now carries a genuine in-pack PLUnit suite - two hundred seventy-two test blocks with four hundred fifty-two output assertions, no trivially-passing tests, full English-Readable-Code - written to mirror the passing legacy acceptance suites where they existed. The per-pack regression grows from two hundred fifty-eight to two hundred ninety-eight packs, all green; the naming linter still reports zero violations.

SPARC: Specification v405, Pseudocode v397, Architecture v398, Refinement v457, Completion v463.

MERGE GATE — EVERY PACK MUST SHIP AN IN-PACK TEST

bin/check_pack_naming.sh gains a fifth merge-blocking check: a pack must ship an in-pack test/test_<name>.pl. A pack without one never enters the per-pack regression and can rot undetected - which is exactly how the six self-recursive crypto stubs survived in lattice_cryptography. The check runs for every pack, including multi-file ones. With all packs now tested it reports zero violations, and a new pack must carry its PLUnit suite from its first commit.

SPARC: Specification v406, Pseudocode v398, Architecture v399, Refinement v458, Completion v464.

TESTS/prNN REGRESSION RUNNER + pr13 CONTAINED

The legacy acceptance suites under tests/prNN live outside packs/ and so were in no regression - they drifted for years undetected until the 2026-07-15 reconcile. bin/run_pr_tests.sh now runs every tests/prNN suite in its own swipl process with a per-suite timeout, so one hanging integration suite cannot block the run; it reports forty-nine passed, zero failed, zero timed out. The one suite that could not pass, pr13, deadlocks when it installs the real reflex_actors cyclic actors against a live Lattice and then uninstalls them (a lock held by a running actor cycle blocks the uninstalling thread's thread_join); its nine tests are marked blocked with that reason, the cyclic-actor lifecycle remaining covered by the actors pack's own in-pack test, and the underlying concurrency deadlock is filed as its own task.

SPARC: Specification v407, Pseudocode v399, Architecture v400, Refinement v459, Completion v465.

REFLEX-ACTOR SHUTDOWN DEADLOCK FIXED — pr13 UN-BLOCKED

The pr13 acceptance suite deadlocked when it installed the real reflex_actors cyclic actors against a live Lattice and uninstalled them. cyclic_actor created NON-detached threads and cyclic_actor_stop ended in an unbounded thread_join, so a wedged actor cycle goal - stuck under Lattice and sentinel contention where thread_signal's injected throw could not interrupt it - blocked the join forever; and because the threads were non-detached it also blocked SWI's own shutdown, so the process resisted even SIGTERM. Actor shutdown is now robust regardless of the underlying race: actor threads are detached (a wedged one can never block halt or a join), a per-actor stop flag lets the loop exit at its next cycle boundary even if the interrupt is missed, and cyclic_actor_stop replaces the unbounded join with a bounded poll - set the flag, signal to break a current sleep, wait about three seconds, force an abort, wait again - so uninstall always returns. pr13's nine tests are un-blocked and pass; the actors pack's own six tests stay green; two hundred ninety-eight packs green; the tests/prNN runner reports forty-nine passed, zero timed out.

SPARC: Specification v408, Pseudocode v400, Architecture v401, Refinement v460, Completion v466.
